          function selecionaTipoConteudoParaBuscaTextual() {
              //zera o que estiver marcado
              $("#searchBar .options input[type=radio]").removeAttr("checked");
              var inputRadioId = "#type-" + $("#nav").find(".on").attr("id")

                  //default perguntas

    <div class="question-summary-wrapper">
        
        <h2><a title="Ainda vale a pena comprar o iPhone 5c em 2016?                     <script type="text/stache" id="jstache_704434078">
                      
    
    
    
    
    
  <div class="flow-body faq clearfix" role="main">
    <div class="container">
        <div class="faq-item">
            <h6 class="question">What is an Apple ID?</h6>
            <p class="answer">An Apple ID is the personal account you use to access Apple services like the App Store, iTunes Store, iCloud, iMessage, the Apple Online Store, FaceTime, and more. It includes the email address and password you use to sign in, as well as all the contact, payment, and security details that you&rsquo;ll use across Apple services.</p>
        </div>
        <div class="faq-item">
            <h6 class="question">When do I use my Apple ID?</h6>
            <p class="answer">Any time you set up a new device, make a purchase, or use any Apple service, you will be asked to sign in with your Apple ID and password. Once signed in you&rsquo;ll have access to the service and all the personal information in your account.</p>
        </div>
        <div class="faq-item">
            <h6 class="question">How many Apple IDs do I need?</h6>
            <p class="answer">Just one. Use the same Apple ID everywhere you sign in to ensure that all your Apple services and devices work together seamlessly and you can access your personal content from all your devices.</p>
        </div>
        <div class="faq-item">
            <h6 class="question">Can I share an Apple ID with someone else?</h6>
            <p class="answer">Your Apple ID should not be shared with anyone else. It provides access to personal information including contacts, photos, device backups, and more. Sharing your Apple ID with someone else means you are giving them access to all your personal content and may lead to confusion over who actually owns the account. To share iTunes & App Store purchases, photos, a calendar, and more with someone else, try <a href="https://support.apple.com/HT201060" target="_blank" title="Family Sharing">Family Sharing</a>, <a href="https://support.apple.com/HT202786" target="_blank" title="iCloud Photo Sharing">iCloud Photo Sharing</a>, or other easy-to-use sharing features.</p>
        </div>
        <div class="faq-item">
            <h6 class="question">How can I keep my Apple ID secure?</h6>
            <p class="answer">Security and privacy are very important to Apple and we provide a number of ways to secure your Apple ID and protect your privacy including strong passwords, two-factor authentication, and more. Learn more about <a href="https://support.apple.com/HT201303" target="_blank" title="Apple ID and Security">security and your Apple ID</a>.</p>
        </div>
        <p class="info">For more information or help, <a href="https://www.apple.com/support/appleid/" target="_blank" title="Apple Support">visit Apple Support</a>.</p>
    </div>
</div>
                    </script>

                locManager.addString('security-questions.securityQuestion2', 'Security Question 2');

	function appendGallery() {

		if ( $('body').hasClass('append-gallery') ) {
			$('#posts').children('.jq:visible').children('article:last').after( $('#posts').children('article') );
		}

		$('ul.social-icons-list li a.btn-more-mobile').remove();
		$('.pop-share').append('<a href="javascript:void(0)" class="btn-more-mobile icon-more" title="Mais"></a>');

    	$('.info-share-new .btn-close, .overlay-share-new').on('click', function(e){
            e.preventDefault();
		    $('.overlay-share-new').fadeOut();
		    $('.info-share-new').fadeOut();

        });

		$('article .bottom-info').on('click', '.btn-more-mobile', function(e){
		    e.preventDefault();
		    var inputDados = $(this).parents('.bottom-info').find('.urlInput');
		    //recolher o título, link do post e copiar o link do input hidden
		    var title_share = inputDados.attr( "name" ),
	            texto_share = inputDados.attr( "placeholder" ),
	            url_share = inputDados.attr( "value" ),
		        hrefWA = "whatsapp://send?text=" + texto_share,
		        hrefDq = url_share + "#comentarios",
		        texto_mailto = "mailto:destinatario@email.com.br?&body=" + encodeURI(texto_share),
		        hrefORonclick = '';

		    //facebook -> url_share
		    if($(window).width() <= 320){
		        var hrefORonclick = 'href',
			        hrefFb = "https://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=" + url_share,
			        hrefTw = "http://twitter.com/intent/tweet?source=webclient&text="+ texto_share,
			        hrefGp = "https://plus.google.com/share?url=" + url_share,
			        hrefLk = "http://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?mini=true&url=" + url_share;
		    } else{
		        var hrefORonclick = 'onclick';
			        hrefFb = "window.open('https://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=" + url_share + "', '_blank', 'toolbar=0,status=0,width=548,height=325');",
			        hrefTw = "window.open('http://twitter.com/intent/tweet?source=webclient&text="+ texto_share +"', '_blank', 'toolbar=0,status=0,width=548,height=325');",
			        hrefGp = "window.open('https://plus.google.com/share?url=" + url_share + "', '_blank', 'toolbar=0,status=0,width=548,height=325');",
			        hrefLk = "window.open('http://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?mini=true&url=" + url_share + "', '_blank', 'toolbar=0,status=0,width=548,height=325');";
		    }

		    $('.info-share-new .share-list li.facebook a').attr( hrefORonclick, hrefFb);
		    $('.info-share-new .share-list li.twitter a').attr( hrefORonclick, hrefTw);
		    $('.info-share-new .share-list li.google-plus a').attr( hrefORonclick, hrefGp);
		    $('.info-share-new .share-list li.linkedin a').attr('onclick', hrefLk);
		    $('.info-share-new .share-list li.whatsapp a').attr('href', hrefWA);
		    $('.info-share-new .share-list li.btn-comments a').attr('href', hrefDq);
		    //email -> texto_email
		    $('.info-share-new .share-list li.email a').attr('href', texto_mailto);
		    //show overlay & share
		    $('.overlay-share-new').fadeIn();
		    $('.info-share-new').fadeIn();

		});

        $('article').each(function() {
        	console.log('nav');
            var self = $(this),
                selectorInput = $(this).find('.urlInput').val(),
                o = $(this).find('.facebook-count'),
                // c = $(this).find('.twitter-count'),
                e = $(this).find('.google-count');
        	console.log(selectorInput);
        	console.log('-----');
            $.getJSON( 'http://graph.facebook.com/?id=' + selectorInput, function( fbdata ) {
                o.text(fbdata.share.share_count);
            });
            // $.getJSON( 'http://cdn.api.twitter.com/1/urls/count.json?url=' + selectorInput + '&callback=?', function( twitdata ) {
            //     c.text(twitdata.count);
            // });
            $.ajax({
    		  type: 'POST',
    		  url: 'https://clients6.google.com/rpc',
    		  processData: true,
    		  contentType: 'application/json',
    		  data: JSON.stringify({
    		    'method':'pos.plusones.get',
    		        'id':'p',
    		        'params':{
    		            'nolog':true,
    		            'id':selectorInput,
    		            'source':'widget',
    		            'userId':'@viewer',
    		            'groupId':'@self'
    		            },
    		        'jsonrpc':'2.0',
    		        'key':'p',
    		        'apiVersion':'v1'
    		  }),
    		  success: function(response) {
    		    e.text(response.result.metadata.globalCounts.count);
    		  }
    		});

    		// $.ajax({

		setTimeout(function(){
			if ( $('a.disqus-comment-count') ) {

				     $('a.disqus-comment-count').each(function() {
				     	var text = $(this).html().trim().split(" ");

		}, 2000);

		<div class="newsletter-box-feedback open" aria-hidden="true" role="presentation" style="display:none">
			<p>Presque ... Nous devons confirmer votre e-mail. Pour compléter le processus de signature, cliquez sur le lien dans le courrier électronique que nous venons de vous envoyer.</p>
			<p>Adresse de contact <em class="form-email">email@email.com</em> déjà enregistré. Pour mettre à jour le dossier, <a href="javascript:void(0)" target="_blank" class="link-cadastro" title="cliquez ici">cliquez ici</a></p>
		</div><!-- newsletter-box -->


		<script>
			$(function() {
				$('form#newsletter-form').submit(function(e) {
					e.preventDefault();
					var email = $('input#email').val(),
						nome = $('input#nome').val(),
						filtro = /^([\w-]+(?:\.[\w-]+)*)@((?:[\w-]+\.)*\w[\w-]{0,66})\.([a-z]{2,6}(?:\.[a-z]{2})?)$/i;;

					var self = $(this);
					var url = self.attr('action');

					self.find('.btn-submit').addClass('off').prop("disabled", true);

					if (email != "" || nome != "") {
						if (filtro.test(email)) {

							$.post(url, self.serialize(), function(data) {

								if ( data === 'sucesso' ) {
									$(".newsletter-box-feedback").children('p:last').hide();
									$(".newsletter-box").hide();
									$(".newsletter-box-feedback").fadeIn();
									self[0].reset();
								} else {
									var dataJson = JSON.parse(data),
										dataCodigo = dataJson.codigo,
										dataMSG = dataJson.msg;

									if ( dataCodigo === 214 ) {
										var link1 = dataMSG.match(/http[s]?:\/\/[a-zA-Z0-9]{1,}.*"/);
										var link = link1[0].replace('"', '');
										$(".newsletter-box-feedback").children('p:first').hide();
										$(".newsletter-box-feedback").children('p:last').find('.form-email').html(email);
										$(".newsletter-box-feedback").children('p:last').find('.link-cadastro').attr('href', link);
										$(".newsletter-box").hide();
										$(".newsletter-box-feedback").fadeIn();
									} else {
										alert( 'Erro '+dataCodigo+' ao cadastrar o e-mail' );
									}

								}
								self.find('.btn-submit').removeClass('off').prop("disabled", false);
							});

						} else {
							$("#email").val("Este endereço de email não é válido!");
							self.find('.btn-submit').removeClass('off').prop("disabled", false);
							return false;
						} // if regex email
					} else { // if email || nome
						$("#email").val('Digite um email!');
						self.find('.btn-submit').removeClass('off').prop("disabled", false);
						return false;
					}
				});
			})
	</script>

	</div><!-- container -->

<script>
	$(function() {
		$('a.btn-change-src').click(function(e) {
			e.preventDefault();

			var self = $(this),
				src = self.children('img').attr('src'),
				href = self.attr('href'),
				hrefFb = "window.open('https://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=" + href + "', '_blank', 'toolbar=0,status=0,width=548,height=325');",
				hrefTw = "window.open('http://twitter.com/intent/tweet?source=webclient&text=Macedo: "+ href +"', '_blank', 'toolbar=0,status=0,width=548,height=325');",
				hrefGp = "window.open('https://plus.google.com/share?url=" + href + "', '_blank', 'toolbar=0,status=0,width=548,height=325');";

			$('div.lightbox a.icon-facebook').parent().attr('onclick', hrefFb);
			$('div.lightbox a.icon-twitter').parent().attr('onclick', hrefTw);
			$('div.lightbox a.icon-google-plus').parent().attr('onclick', hrefGp);
			$('div.overlay img.lightbox-img').attr('src', src);

			$('header').addClass('fix-zindex');

			$('body > div.box > div.overlay').eq(0).fadeIn(400);
			$('body > div.box > div.overlay').removeClass('zoomin')
		});

		$('.overlay .lightbox').on('click', 'a.btn-close', function(e) {
			e.preventDefault();
			$('div.overlay').fadeOut(300);
			$('div.overlay').addClass('zoomin');
			$('header').removeClass('fix-zindex');
		});

		$('.btn-share-img-mobile').on('click', function(e){
			e.preventDefault();
			$(this).parents('.share-img').next().fadeIn();
			$(this).parents('.share-img').next().next().fadeIn();
		});
	});
</script>

                    <p>Presque ... Nous devons confirmer votre e-mail. Pour compléter le processus de signature, cliquez sur le lien dans le courrier électronique que nous venons de vous envoyer.</p>
                    <p>Votre e-mail est déjà sur la base de données du site.</p>
                </div>
                <form action="http://blogs.universal.org/bispomacedo/fr/newsletter/" id="newsletter-form-modal">
                    <label for="nome-modal">Nom</label>
                    <input type="text" name="nome" id="nome-modal" placeholder="Nom" title="Nom">
                    <label for="email-modal">Ecrivez votre e-mail</label>
                    <input type="email" name="email" id="email-modal" placeholder="Ecrivez votre e-mail" title="Ecrivez votre e-mail">
                    <input type="submit" class="btn-submit" value="Oui, je veux recevoir les articles.">
                </form>
            </div>
            <div class="info-bispo-newsletter">
                <figure>
                    <img src="http://blogs.universal.org/bispomacedo/fr/wp-content/themes/bispomacedo-novo/img/bispo-box-newsletter.jpg" alt="">

                        <p>La Parole de Dieu nous lave, purifie et nous donne de la foi atteindre les faveurs de Dieu.</p>

<script>
    $(function() {
        $('form#newsletter-form-modal').submit(function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            var email = $('input#email-modal').val(),
                nome = $('input#nome-modal').val(),
                filtro = /^([\w-]+(?:\.[\w-]+)*)@((?:[\w-]+\.)*\w[\w-]{0,66})\.([a-z]{2,6}(?:\.[a-z]{2})?)$/i;;

            var self = $(this);
            var url = self.attr('action');

            self.find('.btn-submit').addClass('off').prop("disabled", true);

            if (email != "" || nome != "") {
                if (filtro.test(email)) {

                    $.post(url, self.serialize(), function(data) {

                        if ( data === 'sucesso' ) {
                            $(".newsletter-feedback-modal").children('p:last').hide().parent().slideDown('fast');
                            self[0].reset();
                        } else {
                            var dataJson = JSON.parse(data),
                                dataCodigo = dataJson.codigo,
                                dataMSG = dataJson.msg;

                            if ( dataCodigo === 214 ) {
                                $(".newsletter-feedback-modal").children('p:first').hide().parent().slideDown('fast');
                            } else {
                                alert( 'Erro '+dataCodigo+' ao cadastrar o e-mail' );
                            }
                        }
                        self.find('.btn-submit').removeClass('off').prop("disabled", false);
                    });

                } else {
                    $("#email-modal").val("Este endereço de email não é válido!");
                    self.find('.btn-submit').removeClass('off').prop("disabled", false);
                    return false;
                } // if regex email
            } else { // if email || nome
                $("#email-modal").val('Digite um email!');
                self.find('.btn-submit').removeClass('off').prop("disabled", false);
                return false;
            }
        });

    })
</script>
